<p>Default bundled tool names also appear in <code>model_tools.py:221</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">"web_tools": ["web_search", "web_extract"],
</code></pre>
<p>When web tools are unavailable, <code>model_tools.py:452-462</code> adjusts schema hints so the model does not hallucinate search calls.</p>
<hr>
<h2>2. <code>web_search_tool</code> execution</h2>
<pre><code class="language-python"># 160_hermes-agent/tools/web_tools.py:765-852
def web_search_tool(query: str, limit: int = 5) -> str:
    _ensure_web_plugins_loaded()
    backend = _get_search_backend()
    provider = _wsp_get_provider(backend) or get_active_search_provider()
    if provider is None:
        return json.dumps({"success": False, "error": "No web search provider configured. Run `hermes tools`..."})
    response_data = provider.search(query, limit)
    return json.dumps(response_data, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Returns metadata only</strong> (title, url, description, position) — not full page bodies (<code>:772-773</code>). Use <code>web_extract_tool</code> for content (<code>:872+</code>).</p>
<p><strong>Limit clamping:</strong> <code>limit = min(max(limit, 1), 100)</code> (<code>:800-803</code>).</p>
<p><strong>Interrupt:</strong> respects <code>tools.interrupt.is_interrupted()</code> (<code>:817-819</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. Provider plugin registry</h2>
<p><code>agent/web_search_registry.py</code> documents selection precedence (<code>:10-30</code>):</p>
<ol>
<li><code>web.search_backend</code> / <code>web.extract_backend</code> (per-capability)</li>
<li><code>web.backend</code> (shared)</li>
<li>Single registered+available provider auto-pick</li>
<li>Legacy order: <code>firecrawl</code> → <code>parallel</code> → <code>tavily</code> → <code>exa</code> → <code>searxng</code> → <code>brave-free</code> → <code>ddgs</code></li>
<li><code>None</code> → user-facing setup error</li>
</ol>
<p>Registered plugins (each <code>plugins/web/&#x3C;name>/plugin.yaml</code> + <code>provider.py</code>):</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Plugin</th>
<th>Capability</th>
<th>Config / env</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>exa</code></td>
<td>search + extract</td>
<td><code>EXA_API_KEY</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>firecrawl</code></td>
<td>search + extract</td>
<td><code>FIRECRAWL_API_KEY</code> or Nous tool-gateway</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>tavily</code></td>
<td>search + extract</td>
<td><code>TAVILY_API_KEY</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>parallel</code></td>
<td>search + extract</td>
<td><code>PARALLEL_API_KEY</code></td>
</tr>

<td>search</td>

</tr>

<p>Example manifest (<code>plugins/web/exa/plugin.yaml:1-7</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-yaml">name: web-exa

  - exa
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>4. Backend selection (<code>web_tools.py</code>)</h2>
<p><code>_load_web_config()</code> reads <code>web:</code> from <code>~/.hermes/config.yaml</code> (<code>:117-123</code>).</p>
<p><code>_get_search_backend()</code> / <code>_get_extract_backend()</code> allow <strong>split providers</strong> — e.g. SearXNG for search + Firecrawl for extract (<code>:157-179</code>).</p>
<p><code>_get_backend()</code> env fallback chain (<code>:141-152</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">backend_candidates = (
    ("firecrawl", _has_env("FIRECRAWL_API_KEY") or _is_tool_gateway_ready()),
    ("parallel", _has_env("PARALLEL_API_KEY")),
    ("tavily", _has_env("TAVILY_API_KEY")),
    ("exa", _has_env("EXA_API_KEY")),
    ("searxng", _has_env("SEARXNG_URL")),
    ("brave-free", _has_env("BRAVE_SEARCH_API_KEY")),
    ("ddgs", _ddgs_package_importable()),
)
</code></pre>
<p>CLI setup group: <code>hermes_cli/tools_config.py:56</code> — <code>("web", "🔍 Web Search &#x26; Scraping", "web_search, web_extract")</code>.</p>
<p>Preset tool bundles in <code>hermes_cli/config.py:2582+</code> include both tools in default profiles.</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. <code>web_extract_tool</code></h2>
<p>Async extractor (<code>web_tools.py:872-900</code>) with:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Secret-in-URL block</strong> — <code>agent.redact._PREFIX_RE</code> on raw and URL-decoded URLs (<code>:901-911</code>)</li>
<li><strong>SSRF filter</strong> — private/internal URLs stripped before fetch (<code>:933+</code> region)</li>
<li><strong>LLM summarization</strong> — optional OpenRouter/Gemini compression for long pages (module header <code>:20-22</code>, param <code>use_llm_processing</code>)</li>
<li><strong>Debug session</strong> — <code>WEB_TOOLS_DEBUG=true</code> → <code>logs/web_tools_debug_*.json</code> (<code>:24-27</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p>Extract backend dispatch mirrors search via registry + <code>_get_extract_backend()</code>.</p>
<h3>SSRF and search-only provider errors</h3>
<p><code>web_extract_tool</code> filters URLs through <code>tools.url_safety.is_safe_url</code> before any HTTP (<code>web_tools.py:933-943</code>). Blocked URLs return per-URL error objects without calling providers.</p>
<p>When <code>web.extract_backend</code> points at a <strong>search-only</strong> provider (<code>brave-free</code>, <code>ddgs</code>, <code>searxng</code>), Hermes returns an explicit error instead of silently switching backends (<code>:966-979</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-python">f"{provider.display_name} is a search-only backend and cannot extract URL content. "
"Set web.extract_backend to firecrawl, ..."
</code></pre>
<p>Async vs sync <code>provider.extract()</code> is detected at runtime — coroutines are awaited, sync extractors run inline (<code>:951-957</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. Skills fallback when web toolset unavailable</h2>
<p>Bundled skills can appear when the <code>web</code> toolset is missing — e.g. <code>duckduckgo-search</code> skill uses <code>fallback_for_toolsets: [web]</code> (documented in <code>website/docs/user-guide/features/skills.md:148-159</code>). When <code>FIRECRAWL_API_KEY</code> enables the web toolset, native <code>web_search</code> is preferred and the fallback skill stays hidden.</p>
<p><code>agent/prompt_builder.py:1021-1024</code> evaluates <code>fallback_for_toolsets</code> / <code>fallback_for_tools</code> when assembling skill visibility.</p>
<hr>
<h2>7. Nous Tool Gateway (Firecrawl)</h2>
<p><code>tools/managed_tool_gateway.py</code> (imported at <code>web_tools.py:94-98</code>) routes Firecrawl for paid Nous subscribers when direct API keys are absent. <code>_is_tool_gateway_ready()</code> participates in firecrawl availability (<code>:142</code>).</p>
<p><code>hermes_cli/nous_subscription.py:276</code> reads <code>web.extract_backend</code> for subscription-aware defaults.</p>
<hr>
<h2>8. Auxiliary models for extract/vision</h2>
<p><code>gateway/run.py:858-870</code> bridges auxiliary model overrides — <code>web_extract</code> can use a dedicated provider/model tuple separate from the main chat model (see <code>cli.py:627-641</code> for <code>web_extract</code> auxiliary config schema).</p>
<p><code>hermes_cli/config.py:5511</code> surfaces "Web extract" auxiliary settings in config summaries.</p>
<p>This allows cheaper/faster models for page summarization while keeping the primary agent on a larger model.</p>
<hr>
<h2>9. X search (<code>x_search_tool.py</code>)</h2>
<p>Separate from <code>web_search_tool</code> — uses xAI built-in <strong><code>x_search</code></strong> Responses API tool (<code>tools/x_search_tool.py:1-19</code>).</p>
<p>Registers when <code>XAI_API_KEY</code> or SuperGrok OAuth refresh token works. Returns <code>degraded</code> flag when filters active but no citations (<code>:32-37</code>).</p>
<p>Dedicated toolset <code>x_search</code> — off by default; enable via <code>hermes tools</code> (<code>toolsets.py:102-110</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>10. Browser + CDP (adjacent)</h2>
<p><code>tools/browser_tool.py:1-25</code> — agent-browser CLI (local Chromium or Browserbase/Browser Use cloud).</p>
<p><code>browser</code> toolset embeds <code>web_search</code> for URL discovery before navigation (<code>toolsets.py:170-178</code>).</p>
<p><code>tools/browser_cdp_tool.py</code> — CDP escape hatch for targets inaccessible via accessibility tree.</p>
<h3>Browser + search workflow</h3>
<p>Typical agent pattern encoded in toolset design:</p>
<ol>
<li><code>web_search(query)</code> → candidate URLs (metadata JSON)</li>
<li><code>browser_navigate(url)</code> or <code>web_extract(urls)</code> depending on need</li>
<li><code>browser_snapshot</code> / <code>browser_click</code> for interactive pages</li>
</ol>
<p><code>browser</code> toolset explicitly lists <code>web_search</code> alongside eleven <code>browser_*</code> actions (<code>toolsets.py:172-177</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>11. Gateway / CLI integration</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Surface</th>
<th>Path</th>
<th>Role</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Tool wizard</td>
<td><code>hermes_cli/tools_config.py</code></td>
<td>Interactive provider setup</td>
</tr>
<tr>

Tool Gateway doc (<code>tool-gateway.md</code>) describes Nous-hosted Firecrawl for subscribers without separate API keys.</p>

<h3>Why Hermes ranks "broad" on web/search axis</h3>
<p>Hermes combines <strong>provider-pluggable API search</strong>, <strong>LLM-compressed extract</strong>, <strong>X index search</strong>, and <strong>browser automation</strong> in one process. Most harnesses implement at most two of these (e.g. <code>cc</code>: WebSearch + WebFetch; <code>omo</code>: MCP Exa only; <code>co</code>: Responses <code>web_search</code> only).</p>
<hr>
<h2>14. End-to-end flow</h2>
<pre><code>User/agent → web_search(query)
  → _get_search_backend() from config.yaml
  → web_search_registry.get_provider(name)
  → plugins/web/&#x3C;backend>/provider.search(query, limit)
  → JSON { success, data: { web: [{title, url, description}] } }
  → (optional) web_extract(urls) for full text + LLM summary
</code></pre>
<h3>JSON result shape (search)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-json">{
  "success": true,
  "data": {
    "web": [
      { "title": "...", "url": "https://...", "description": "...", "position": 1 }
    ]
  }
}
</code></pre>
<p>Documented in <code>web_search_tool</code> docstring (<code>web_tools.py:779-794</code>).</p>

<h2>소스 코드 스니펫</h2>
<h3><code>160_hermes-agent/README.md</code></h3>
<h2>Quick Install</h2>
<h3>Linux, macOS, WSL2, Termux</h3>
<pre><code class="language-bash">curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/NousResearch/hermes-agent/main/scripts/install.sh | bash
</code></pre>
<h3>Windows (native, PowerShell) — Early Beta</h3>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>Heads up:</strong> Native Windows support is <strong>early beta</strong>. It installs and runs, but hasn't been road-tested as broadly as our Linux/macOS/WSL2 paths. Please <a href="https://github.com/NousResearch/hermes-agent/issues">file issues</a> when you hit rough edges. For the most battle-tested Windows setup today, run the Linux/macOS one-liner above inside <strong>WSL2</strong>.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Run this in PowerShell:</p>
<pre><code class="language-powershell">iex (irm https://raw.githubusercontent.com/NousResearch/hermes-agent/main/scripts/install.ps1)
</code></pre>
<p>The installer handles everything: uv, Python 3.11, Node.js, ripgrep, ffmpeg, <strong>and a portable Git Bash</strong> (MinGit, unpacked to <code>%LOCALAPPDATA%\hermes\git</code> — no admin required, completely isolated from any system Git install).  Hermes uses this bundled Git Bash to run shell commands.</p>
<p>If you already have Git installed, the installer detects it and uses that instead.  Otherwise a ~45MB MinGit download is all you need — it won't touch or interfere with any system Git.</p>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>Android / Termux:</strong> The tested manual path is documented in the <a href="https://hermes-agent.nousresearch.com/docs/getting-started/termux">Termux guide</a>. On Termux, Hermes installs a curated <code>.[termux]</code> extra because the full <code>.[all]</code> extra currently pulls Android-incompatible voice dependencies.</p>
<p><strong>Windows:</strong> Native Windows is supported as an <strong>early beta</strong> — the PowerShell one-liner above installs everything, but expect rough edges and please file issues when you hit them. If you'd rather use WSL2 (our most battle-tested Windows path), the Linux command works there too. Native Windows install lives under <code>%LOCALAPPDATA%\hermes</code>; WSL2 installs under <code>~/.hermes</code> as on Linux.  The only Hermes feature that currently needs WSL2 specifically is the browser-based dashboard chat pane (it uses a POSIX PTY — classic CLI and gateway both run natively).</p>
</blockquote>
<p>After installation:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">source ~/.bashrc    # reload shell (or: source ~/.zshrc)
hermes              # start chatting!
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>코퍼스 — 015_reverse-engineering/ (심화)</h2>
<h3><code>015_reverse-engineering/00_reverse_evidence_policy.md</code></h3>
<h1>Reverse Engineering Evidence Policy</h1>
<p>이 축은 설치 help parity 문서의 다음 단계다. 기존 <code>00</code>~<code>14</code> 축은 주로 help/config/local-doc 표면을 비교했고, 이 축은 설치된 바이너리와 번들에서 복원 가능한 구조를 따로 기록한다.</p>
<h2>Evidence Levels</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Level</th>
<th>의미</th>
<th>사용할 수 있는 주장</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>installed-help</td>
<td><code>--help</code>, public command output, version output</td>
<td>명령/플래그/공개 subcommand가 존재한다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>safe-local-doc</td>
<td>설치 패키지의 docs, changelog, examples, manifest</td>
<td>문서화된 schema/경로/기능 설명이 있다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>bundle-key</td>
<td>minified bundle에 남은 module key, source path, route name, proto name</td>
<td>내부 모듈/라우터/프로토/컴포넌트가 존재한다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>binary-string</td>
<td>native binary <code>strings</code>, <code>file</code>, <code>otool</code>, <code>codesign</code>, <code>nm</code></td>
<td>crate/package/protocol/tool/evaluator 이름이 embedded되어 있다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>runtime-trace</td>
<td>synthetic project에서 실제 명령을 실행한 결과</td>
<td>동작 semantics, precedence, permission enforcement를 확인했다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>private-artifact-name</td>
<td>비공개 상태 파일의 경로/개수만 관찰</td>
<td>artifact가 존재한다. 내용/schema 주장은 금지</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/015_reverse-engineering/33_source_deobfuscation_inventory.md</code> further separates source-like recovery levels. In this corpus, Cursor reaches preserved module-key recovery, while Grok/Kiro/AGY mostly expose native source-path, handler, protobuf, and runtime-trace evidence. Do not call this "full source recovered" unless a real source map or readable source archive is present.</p>
<h2>Hard Boundary</h2>
<p>역분석의 목적은 제품 구조 복원이지 사용자 상태 추출이 아니다. 다음은 내용 읽기 금지다.</p>
<ul>
<li>auth/token/cookie/credential/login data</li>
<li>raw transcript, chat history, conversation DB/PB</li>
<li>logs and terminal captures</li>
<li>browser profile state, local storage, IndexedDB, session storage</li>
<li>memory/goal runtime stores</li>
<li>screenshots and browser recordings</li>
<li>private <code>mcp.json</code>, settings, config values unless explicitly redacted</li>
</ul>
<p>비공개 artifact는 “존재한다”까지만 쓴다. 필드/schema/content 주장은 public docs, source/bundle evidence, sanitized fixture, synthetic runtime trace가 있을 때만 쓴다.</p>
<h2>Installed CLI version pin (2026-06-27)</h2>
<p>Single source of truth for pinned <code>ay</code>/<code>cr</code>/<code>gr</code>/<code>ki</code> binaries:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/015_reverse-engineering/36_installed_cli_version_manifest.md</code></li>
</ul>
<p>WP5 trace shards (<code>38</code>–<code>41</code>) extend hubs without changing evidence-level definitions above.</p>

<h2>Reading Rule For Existing Docs</h2>
<p>When a <code>00</code>~<code>14</code> page says “없음” or “지원하지 않음”, interpret it as “installed help에서 노출되지 않음” unless this <code>15_reverse-engineering</code> axis confirms absence from bundle/binary evidence too.</p>
<p>When a page states runtime semantics from config/cache observation, this axis upgrades or downgrades the claim:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>bundle-key</code> or <code>binary-string</code> confirms a module exists.</li>
<li><code>runtime-trace</code> is still required for exact precedence, scheduling, isolation, merge, and permission behavior.</li>
</ul>

<li>2026-05-29: Hermes Agent(<code>NousResearch/hermes-agent</code>, v0.15.1) 동작 원리 최초 작성. 4종 진입점(CLI/TUI/Gateway/ACP), HERMES_HOME 프로파일 경로, 3-로더 설정, ~20플랫폼 다채널 게이트웨이(platform_registry/base/_handle_message/SessionResetPolicy/AIAgent LRU 캐시/COMMAND_REGISTRY 자동파생), registry+toolsets 2단계 도구 모델 + _HERMES_CORE_TOOLS 표 + 환경 백엔드 + MCP 양방향, 3계층 시스템 프롬프트(frozen-snapshot prefix 캐시 불변식), 영속·자기개선 메모리(MEMORY.md/USER.md + MemoryManager 플러그인 + SessionDB SQLite/FTS5/trigram + Curator 자기개선 루프), 동기 run_conversation 루프 + 멀티 프로토콜 어댑터/모델 라우팅 + delegate_task 서브에이전트, 턴 생존 실행(cron/background/queue/steer/handoff), 보안(tirith/승인/미디어 denylist/셸 훅), ACP 어댑터, 플러그인·스킬 생태계, 관찰성, cli-jaw 6항목 비교 포함.</li>
</ul>
<h2>000/00_grand_synthesis.md (발췌)</h2>
<h1>GRAND SYNTHESIS — 5개 코딩 에이전트 × 13개 차원 최종 종합 분석</h1>
<p>이 문서는 Codex, Aider, Gemini CLI, OpenCode, Claude Code를 13개 아키텍처 차원에서 동시에 비교한 캡스톤 문서다.
개별 비교 문서의 결론을 단순 재배열하지 않고, 서로 다른 설계 철학이 어떤 제품 전략으로 수렴하는지까지 읽어내는 것을 목표로 한다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD
    A[5개 에이전트 개요] --> B[13개 차원 비교]
    B --> C[공통 패턴 추출]
    B --> D[핵심 차별점 추출]
    C --> E[기술 선택 시사점]
    D --> E
    E --> F[미래 전망과 설계 교훈]
</code></pre>
<h2>1. 개요</h2>
<h3>이 문서의 목적</h3>
<p>이 문서의 목적은 5개 에이전트를 한 번에 조망할 수 있는 상위 레퍼런스를 만드는 것이다.
개별 문서는 특정 축의 우열을 설명하지만, 실제 제품 선택은 언제나 여러 축의 동시 판단을 요구한다.
따라서 여기서는 TUI, prompt, tool, skill, subagent, app-server, sandbox, config, MCP, memory, plugin, guardian, 그리고 잔여 교차 관심사를 하나의 프레임으로 다시 묶는다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[00_ai_overview]], [[00_ge_overview]], [[00_oc_overview]], [[00_cc_overview]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>분석 범위</h3>
<p>범위는 5개 에이전트와 13개 차원이다.
에이전트는 Codex, Aider, Gemini CLI, OpenCode, Claude Code다.
차원은 TUI, Prompt/Context, Tool Runtime, Skill, Subagents, App-Server Surface, Sandbox, Config, MCP, Memory, Plugin, Guardian, 잔여 교차 관심사(Git/VCS, 모델 라우팅, 에러 처리, 텔레메트리, IDE 통합, 패키징, 테스트, 인증, 멀티모달, 이벤트 시스템, 피처 플래그, 국제화)다.
App-Server 축은 비교 문서 자체가 Codex·Gemini CLI·OpenCode 중심으로 작성되어 있으므로 Aider와 Claude Code는 “의도적 부재”까지 함께 해석한다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[002_prompt-context/00_prompt]], [[003_tool-runtime/00_tool]], [[004_skill-system/00_skill]], [[005_subagents-collab/00_subagent]], [[006_app-server-client-surfaces/00_surface]], [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[008_config-system/00_config]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]], [[010_memory-pipeline/00_memory]], [[011_plugin-system/00_plugin]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]], [[013_etc/00_etc]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>분석 방법론</h3>
<p>첫째, 각 에이전트 개요 문서에서 기술 스택, 패키지 구조, 핵심 철학을 추출했다.
둘째, 13개 비교 문서에서 축별 우위와 결손, 스카우팅 점수, 디자인 패턴을 수집했다.
셋째, 같은 에이전트가 여러 축에서 반복적으로 보이는 패턴을 묶어 장기 전략으로 재해석했다.
넷째, 단일 승자를 찾기보다 “어떤 상황에서 어떤 설계가 더 설득력 있는가”를 기준으로 실무 추천안을 도출했다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[00_ai_overview]], [[00_ge_overview]], [[00_oc_overview]], [[00_cc_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>이 문서를 읽는 방법</h3>
<p>제품 선택이 목적이면 3장, 7장, 8장을 먼저 보는 것이 좋다.
포크나 재구현이 목적이면 2장, 5장, 6장, 9장을 먼저 보는 것이 좋다.
보안 검토가 목적이면 3장, 4장, 8장, 9장을 함께 읽는 편이 낫다.
마지막 부록은 문서 인덱스 역할을 하므로 세부 원문으로 돌아갈 때 사용하면 된다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]], [[011_plugin-system/00_plugin]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]]</li>
</ul>

<tr>
<td>Codex</td>
<td>Rust + TypeScript + React/Ink + app-server protocol</td>
<td>엔진을 층으로 분리하고, prompt·tool·skill·subagent·MCP를 제어면(control plane)으로 다룬다.</td>
<td>가장 분해 가능한 core engine, 가장 강한 terminal-native orchestration, 가장 균형 잡힌 sandbox/MCP 결합.</td>
<td>보안, 오케스트레이션, 포크 가능한 core engine이 중요한 팀</td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td>Aider</td>
<td>Python + prompt_toolkit + rich + tree-sitter + Git</td>
<td>도구 플랫폼보다 코드 편집 루프에 집중한다. 모델을 좋은 editor로 만드는 쪽에 최적화한다.</td>
<td>RepoMap, edit 전략 다양성, git auto-commit, 최소 마찰 CLI 경험.</td>
<td>개인 개발자, 빠른 코드 편집, 낮은 학습 비용이 중요한 사용 사례</td>
<td>[[00_ai_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[002_prompt-context/00_prompt]]</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gemini CLI</td>
<td>TypeScript + React/Ink + Zod + A2A server + multi-package monorepo</td>
<td>schema-first와 policy-first를 결합해 CLI를 확장 운영체계처럼 다룬다.</td>
<td>PromptProvider/Scheduler/PolicyEngine/ModelRouter/ExtensionManager가 분리된 가장 운영형 TypeScript engine.</td>
<td>엔터프라이즈 CLI, 확장 운영, 정책 감사, TypeScript 기반 재구현</td>
<td>[[00_ge_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[004_skill-system/00_skill]]</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>OpenCode</td>
<td>TypeScript + Bun + Effect-TS + Hono + SolidJS + Tauri</td>
<td>agent runtime을 웹/데스크톱/SDK가 공유하는 product platform으로 본다.</td>
<td>Effect-TS service layer, 21+ provider, plugin SDK, session replay, multi-surface delivery.</td>
<td>빠른 제품화, GUI/desktop 포함, TS로 직접 확장하고 싶은 팀</td>
<td>[[00_oc_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[003_tool-runtime/00_tool]]</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Claude Code</td>
<td>TypeScript/JavaScript bundle + React/Ink + custom renderer + Anthropic runtime</td>
<td>제품 사용성을 최우선으로 하면서 hook, security chain, memory, MCP를 깊게 묶는다.</td>
<td>가장 풍부한 productized tool surface, deepest shell security, strongest file-based memory UX.</td>
<td>상용 CLI UX, 강한 shell security, memory-heavy workflows, enterprise policy integration</td>
<td>[[00_cc_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[005_subagents-collab/00_subagent]]</td>
</tr>

<h3>Codex</h3>
<ul>
<li>정체성: 엔진을 층으로 분리하고, prompt·tool·skill·subagent·MCP를 제어면(control plane)으로 다룬다.</li>
<li>기술 스택: Rust + TypeScript + React/Ink + app-server protocol</li>
<li>핵심 차별점: 가장 분해 가능한 core engine, 가장 강한 terminal-native orchestration, 가장 균형 잡힌 sandbox/MCP 결합.</li>
<li>실무에서 강한 상황: 보안, 오케스트레이션, 포크 가능한 core engine이 중요한 팀</li>
<li>재구현 관점 한 줄 평: requirements 제약 채널과 prompt fragment provenance를 분리한 구조.</li>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[002_prompt-context/00_prompt]], [[003_tool-runtime/00_tool]], [[005_subagents-collab/00_subagent]], [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>Aider</h3>
<ul>
<li>정체성: 도구 플랫폼보다 코드 편집 루프에 집중한다. 모델을 좋은 editor로 만드는 쪽에 최적화한다.</li>
<li>기술 스택: Python + prompt_toolkit + rich + tree-sitter + Git</li>
<li>핵심 차별점: RepoMap, edit 전략 다양성, git auto-com</li>
</ul>
